Abstract: Generative policies based on expressive model classes, such as diffusion and flow matching, are well-suited to complex control problems with highly multimodal action distributions. Their expressivity, however, comes at a significant inference cost: generating each action typically requires simulating many steps of the generative process, compounding latency across sequential decision-making rollouts. We introduce flow map policies, a novel class of generative policies designed for fast action generation by learning to take arbitrary-size jumps including one-step jumps-across the generative dynamics of existing flow-based policies. We instantiate flow map policies for offline-to-online reinforcement learning (RL) and formulate online adaptation as a trust-region optimization problem that improves the critic's Q-value while remaining close to the offline policy. We theoretically derive FLOW MAP Q-GUIDANCE (FMQ), a principled closed-form learning target that is optimal for adapting offline flow map policies under a critic-guided trust-region constraint. We further introduce Q-GUIDED BEAM SEARCH (QGBS), a stochastic flow-map sampler that combines renoising with beam search to enable iterative inference-time refinement. Across 12 challenging robotic manipulation and locomotion tasks from OGBench and RoboMimic, FMQ achieves state-of-the-art performance in offline-to-online RL, outperforming the previous one-step policy MVP by a relative improvement of 21.3% on the average success rate.

Abstract: For minimally rigid graphs, the same edge-length data can admit multiple realizations (up to translations and rotations). However, existing verbalized-confidence methods often optimize answer generation and confidence generation jointly, which can cause confidence-alignment objectives to interfere with answer accuracy. In this work, we propose a decoupled and order-aware framework for verbalized confidence calibration. Our method first generates an answer and then estimates confidence conditioned on the fixed question--answer pair, allowing confidence optimization without directly perturbing the answer-generation process. ### [219] [Multi-Stream LLMs: Unblocking Language Models with Parallel Streams of Thoughts, Inputs and Outputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12460)
*Guinan Su,Yanwu Yang,Xueyan Li,Jonas Geiping*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将语言模型从单流消息格式转变为多流并行计算范式，通过为每个角色分配独立的数据流，使模型能同时进行读取、思考、写作和行动，从而突破传统聊天模型的计算瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI智能体基于顺序消息交换格式（如ChatGPT），存在单流计算瓶颈：无法同时读写、无法边思考边行动，限制了智能体的效率、安全性和可用性。

Method: 从指令微调顺序消息格式转向指令微调多路并行流格式，将每个角色（用户、系统、模型自身、工具）拆分为独立的数据流，每次前向传播同时从多个输入流读取并在多个输出流生成token。

Result: 多流并行计算能够：1) 解决单流瓶颈限制；2) 通过并行化提升模型效率；3) 通过关注点分离改善安全性；4) 提升模型可监控性。

Conclusion: 通过数据驱动的方式改变模型的计算范式（从单流到多流），可以显著改善AI智能体的可用性、效率、安全性和可监控性。

Abstract: The continued improvements in language model capability have unlocked their widespread use as drivers of autonomous agents, for example in coding or computer use applications. However, the core of these systems has not changed much since early instruction-tuned models like ChatGPT. Even advanced AI agents function on message exchange formats, successively exchanging messages with users, systems, with itself (i.e. chain-of-thought) and tools in a single stream of computation. This bottleneck to a single stream in chat models leads to a number of limitations: the agent cannot act (generate output) while reading, and in reverse, cannot react to new information while writing. Similarly, the agent cannot act while thinking and cannot think while reading or acting on information.
  In this work, we show that models can be unblocked by switching from instruction-tuning for sequential message formats to instruction-tuning for multiple, parallel streams of computation, splitting each role into a separate stream. Every forward pass of the language model then simultaneously reads from multiple input streams and generates tokens in multiple output streams, all of which causally depend on earlier timesteps. We argue that this data-driven change remedies a number of usability limitations as outlined above, improves model efficiency through parallelization, improves model security through better separation of concerns and can further improve model monitorability.

</details>


### [220] [High-arity Sample Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12465)
*Leonardo N. Coregliano,William Opich*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将学习理论中的概念扩展到乘积空间（高元学习理论），并探索高元样本压缩方案与PAC可学习性之间的关系。

Method: 提出了高元样本压缩方案的概念，并通过理论证明建立其与非平凡质量及高元PAC可学习性之间的联系。

Result: 证明了非平凡质量的高元样本压缩方案的存在性蕴含高元PAC可学习性。

Conclusion: 高元样本压缩方案是高元PAC可学习性的一个充分条件，为高元学习理论提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Recently, a series of works have started studying variations of concepts from learning theory for product spaces, which can be collected under the name high-arity learning theory. In this work, we consider a high-arity variant of sample compression schemes and we prove that the existence of a high-arity sample compression scheme of non-trivial quality implies high-arity PAC learnability.

### [221] [Solve the Loop: Attractor Models for Language and Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12466)
*Jacob Fein-Ashley,Paria Rashidinejad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Attractor Models，通过隐式微分求解不动点来替代传统循环Transformer，在语言建模和推理任务上均取得显著提升，并能将迭代计算内化到模型参数中，推理时可移除迭代过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环Transformer虽能迭代精炼表征，但存在训练不稳定、优化部署成本高、受限于固定小深度等问题。作者希望设计一种可扩展的迭代精炼机制，既能享受深度迭代的好处，又能避免传统循环架构的缺陷。

Method: 提出Attractor Models：主干模块先提出输出嵌入，吸引子模块通过求解不动点来精炼嵌入，梯度通过隐式微分获得。这样训练内存与有效深度无关，迭代次数由收敛性自适应决定。

Result: 语言建模：困惑度提升高达46.6%，下游准确率提升19.7%；770M模型超越在双倍数据上训练的1.3B Transformer。推理任务：27M参数模型在Sudoku-Extreme达91.4%，Maze-Hard达93.1%，远超Claude/GPT o3和专用递归推理器。此外发现平衡内化现象，推理时可移除求解器。

Conclusion: Attractor Models通过将循环转化为模型可内化的计算，使迭代精炼变得可扩展，在性能和效率上均实现帕累托改进。

Abstract: Looped Transformers offer a promising alternative to purely feed-forward computation by iteratively refining latent representations, improving language modeling and reasoning. Yet recurrent architectures remain unstable to train, costly to optimize and deploy, and constrained to small, fixed recurrence depths. We introduce Attractor Models, in which a backbone module first proposes output embeddings, then an attractor module refines them by solving for the fixed point, with gradients obtained through implicit differentiation. Thus, training memory remains constant in effective depth, and iterations are chosen adaptively by convergence. Empirically, Attractor Models outperform existing models across two regimes, large-scale language-model pretraining and reasoning with tiny models. In language modeling, Attractor Models deliver a Pareto improvement over standard Transformers and stable looped models across sizes, improving perplexity by up to 46.6% and downstream accuracy by up to 19.7% while reducing training cost. Notably, a 770M Attractor Model outperforms a 1.3B Transformer trained on twice as many tokens. On challenging reasoning tasks, we show that our model with only 27M parameters and approximately 1000 examples achieves 91.4% accuracy on Sudoku-Extreme and 93.1% on Maze-Hard, scaling favorably where frontier models like Claude and GPT o3, fail completely, and specialized recursive reasoners collapse at larger sizes. Lastly, we show that Attractor Models exhibit a novel phenomenon, which we call equilibrium internalization: fixed-point training places the model's initial output embedding near equilibrium, allowing the solver to be removed at inference time with little degradation. Together, these results suggest that Attractor Models make iterative refinement scalable by turning recurrence into a computation the model can learn to internalize.

</details>


### [222] [KV-Fold: One-Step KV-Cache Recurrence for Long-Context Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12471)
*Alireza Nadali,Patrick Cooper,Ashutosh Trivedi,Alvaro Velasquez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KV-Fold是一种无需训练的长上下文推理协议，将KV缓存作为序列块递归累加器，通过类似函数式编程中foldl的方式实现稳定递归，在128K上下文和511层链深度下实现100%精确检索，且仅需单张40GB GPU。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文推理方法存在内存限制或需要模型修改/重新训练，作者希望寻找一种无需训练、不改变模型架构的实用长上下文推理方案。

Method: 将KV缓存视为左折叠(foldl)中的累加器，逐块处理序列：处理当前块时，模型关注之前块累积的KV缓存作为前缀，将新产生的KV追加到缓存中传递给下一块，形成块到块的递归。

Result: 在Llama-3.1-8B上，从16K到128K上下文的152次试验中实现100%精确检索；递归稳定，每步漂移短暂上升后趋于平坦，对数值精度(10000倍变化)、块大小和模型家族均不敏感；可在单张40GB GPU内运行。

Conclusion: 预训练的冻结Transformer已经支持稳定的KV缓存递归形式，无需架构改变或训练即可实现长上下文推理。

Abstract: We introduce KV-Fold, a simple, training-free long-context inference protocol that treats the key-value (KV) cache as the accumulator in a left fold over sequence chunks. At each step, the model processes the next chunk conditioned on the accumulated cache, appends the newly produced keys and values, and passes the enlarged cache forward; the same one-step update is applied repeatedly, analogous to foldl in functional programming. Building on the KV cache concatenation primitive introduced for latent multi-agent communication, we repurpose it as a chunk-to-chunk recurrence for long-context inference. When processing chunk t, the model attends to the KV cache carried from earlier chunks as a prefix, reusing its internal state across segments without modifying or retraining the model. Despite its simplicity, the induced recurrence is stable: per-step drift rises briefly and then saturates into a flat plateau that persists across deep chains. This plateau is insensitive to a 10,000x change in numerical precision, robust across chunk sizes, and consistent across model families. At the task level, KV-Fold preserves exact information over long distances. On a needle-in-a-haystack benchmark, it achieves 100% exact-match retrieval across 152 trials spanning contexts from 16K to 128K tokens and chain depths up to 511 on Llama-3.1-8B, while remaining within the memory limits of a single 40GB GPU. Compared to streaming methods, which trade fidelity for bounded memory, KV-Fold maintains long-range retrieval while operating as a sequence of tractable forward passes. Overall, our results show that frozen pretrained transformers already support a stable form of KV-cache recurrence, providing a practical route to long-context inference without architectural changes or training.

</details>


### [223] [Routers Learn the Geometry of Their Experts: Geometric Coupling in Sparse Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12476)
*Sagi Ahrac,Noya Hochwald,Mor Geva*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了SMoE模型中路由器与对应专家之间存在几何耦合关系：路由器权重和专家权重的梯度沿相同输入方向累积，形成共享的历史信息。辅助负载均衡损失会破坏这种耦合，而基于K-Means的无参数路由器能更好地保持几何耦合，实现低负载失衡与可接受的困惑度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SMoE模型训练中存在路由坍缩和辅助负载均衡损失降低专家 specialization 的问题，现有方法缺乏对路由决策机制的理解。

Method: 1）理论分析路由器与专家之间的几何耦合关系；2）实验验证1B SMoE模型中的耦合现象（高路由器分数对应强专家激活）；3）分析辅助负载均衡损失对耦合的破坏作用；4）提出参数无关的在线K-Means路由器，用余弦相似度分配token。

Result: 1）路由器与专家的梯度沿相同输入方向累积；2）路由器分数与专家神经元激活强度正相关；3）辅助负载均衡损失使路由器方向相似度提升近3倍；4）K-Means路由器在最低负载失衡下仅适度增加困惑度。

Conclusion: 几何耦合是SMoE有效路由的核心机制，路由器形成支持有效分工的分配几何结构，为设计更好的路由策略提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (SMoE) models enable scaling language models efficiently, but training them remains challenging, as routing can collapse onto few experts and auxiliary load-balancing losses can reduce specialization. Motivated by these hurdles, we study how routing decisions in SMoEs are formed mechanistically. First, we reveal a geometric coupling between routers and their corresponding experts. For a given token, the router weights for the selected expert and the expert weights processing it receive gradients along the same input direction, differing only in scalar coefficients. Thus, matched router--expert directions accumulate the same routed token history. This theoretical coupling also appears empirically in routing dynamics. In a $1$B SMoE trained from scratch, higher router scores predict stronger expert neuron activations, showing that routing decisions are mirrored inside the selected expert. Next, we analyze the effects of auxiliary load balancing on the router--expert geometric coupling, showing that such losses break this structure by spreading input-directed gradients across router weights, making distinct router directions nearly three times more similar to each other. Last, we demonstrate the centrality of geometric coupling for effective routing with a parameter-free online K-Means router, in which each expert maintains a running average of the hidden states routed to it and tokens are assigned based on cosine similarity. Compared with auxiliary-loss and loss-free balancing, this router achieves the lowest load imbalance with only a modest perplexity increase, indicating that geometric coupling captures a substantial part of what the router learns. Overall, our results explain how routers form assignment geometry that supports an effective division of labor.

</details>

*Seokwon Jung,Alexander Rubinstein,Arnas Uselis,Sangdoo Yun,Seong Joon Oh*

TL;DR: MEME基准测试提出了多实体、演化记忆的六类任务，发现现有记忆系统在依赖推理任务上严重失效（准确率仅1-3%），即使优化也无法解决，只有高成本方案能部分改善。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 定义了六类任务（含Cascade、Absence、Deletion三类新任务），在100个受控故事场景中，评测了六种跨三类范式的记忆系统，并进行提示优化、检索深度、噪声控制等消融实验。

Result: 所有系统在依赖推理任务上近乎崩溃（Cascade: 3%, Absence: 1%）；多数优化策略（更强LLM、提示优化等）均无法弥补这一差距；仅Claude Opus 4.7 + 文件代理方案能部分解决，但成本高达基线70倍。

Abstract: LLM-based agents increasingly operate in persistent environments where they must store, update, and reason over information across many sessions. While prior benchmarks evaluate only single-entity updates, MEME defines six tasks spanning the full space defined by the multi-entity and evolving axes, including three not scored by prior work: Cascade and Absence (dependency reasoning) and Deletion (post-removal state). Evaluating six memory systems spanning three memory paradigms on 100 controlled episodes, we find that all systems collapse on dependency reasoning under the default configuration (Cascade: 3%, Absence: 1% in average accuracy) despite adequate static retrieval performance. Prompt optimization, deeper retrieval, reduced filler noise, and most stronger LLMs fail to close this gap. Only a file-based agent paired with Claude Opus 4.7 as its internal LLM partially closes the gap, but at ~70x the baseline cost, indicating closure currently depends on configurations that are not practical at scale. Code and data are available on the project page: https://seokwonjung-jay.github.io/meme-eval/.

### [225] [Beyond GRPO and On-Policy Distillation: An Empirical Sparse-to-Dense Reward Principle for Language-Model Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12483)
*Yuanda Xu,Hejian Sang,Zhengze Zhou,Ran He,Zhipeng Wang,Alborz Geramifard*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出应遵循"奖励密度原则"合理分配稀缺的标注验证数据：将稀疏奖励用于强模型的探索（如GRPO），再通过稠密监督（如OPD）将行为压缩到小模型，而非直接在部署学生模型上使用稀疏RL。在数学推理任务上的实验验证了这一分配规则的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前标准做法是将稀缺的带标签验证数据直接用于最终部署的小模型（如在其上运行GRPO），但这种分配效率低下。作者认为需要根据奖励密度原则重新思考数据分配策略。

Method: 提出一种"上游探索+下游压缩"的两阶段方法：先用稀疏序列级奖励（GRPO风格）在强教师模型上进行探索和奖励塑造，再通过稠密token级教师监督（OPD风格）将行为转移到学生模型。关键设计包括前向KL预热和学生rollout上的OPD，形成"桥接"（bridge）。

Result: 在Qwen3和Llama模型上的数学推理实验表明：1) RL增强的8B教师通过稠密桥接蒸馏优于直接在1.7B学生上运行GRPO；2) 桥接后学生侧GRPO可从75.4%提升至78.5%，超过对照2.8个百分点；3) 前向KL预热+学生rollout上OPD的组合在MATH上表现最强。

Conclusion: 核心操作原则是：不要将稀缺标注数据浪费在最不成熟的策略上。稀疏奖励应用于教师侧的探索发现，稠密转移用于学生侧的压缩，学生侧的稀疏奖励只有在桥接之后才有效。

Abstract: In settings where labeled verifiable training data is the binding constraint, each checked example should be allocated carefully. The standard practice is to use this data directly on the model that will be deployed, for example by running GRPO on the deployment student. We argue that this is often an inefficient allocation because it overlooks a reward-density principle: sparse sequence-level reward should train models where exploration is productive, while dense token-level teacher reward should be used where the aim is to compress behavior into a smaller model. In this view, GRPO-style sparse RL and OPD-style dense teacher supervision are not separate recipes; they are different reward-density regimes. The allocation rule is simple: use scarce labeled training data upstream on the strongest model that can turn it into reward-shaped behavior, then transfer that behavior downstream as dense supervision. We evaluate this rule on verifiable math with Qwen3 and Llama models. At fixed Qwen3-1.7B deployment-student size, an RL-improved 8B teacher distilled through the dense bridge outperforms direct GRPO on the same student, while transfer from the same teacher before RL underperforms. The bridge is important: a forward-KL warmup on teacher rollouts followed by OPD on student rollouts is consistently strongest on MATH before any post-bridge student-side sparse RL, and also gives the best pre-Stage~3 AIME endpoints for the canonical 8B/14B teachers. The bridge also makes later student-side sparse RL effective: GRPO that is weak on a cold student lifts MATH from $75.4\%$ to $78.5\%$ after the bridge and outperforms a matched replay control by $2.8$ points. The operational principal is to avoid using scarce labeled data on the least prepared policy: use sparse reward for teacher-side discovery, dense transfer for student compression, and student-side sparse reward only after the bridge.

</details>


### [226] [Learning, Fast and Slow: Towards LLMs That Adapt Continually](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12484)
*Rishabh Tiwari,Kusha Sareen,Lakshya A Agrawal,Joseph E. Gonzalez,Matei Zaharia,Kurt Keutzer,Inderjit S Dhillon,Rishabh Agarwal,Devvrit Khatri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Fast-Slow Training (FST)框架，通过将模型参数作为"慢"权重、优化后的上下文作为"快"权重，实现LLM的快速慢速双轨学习。FST在推理任务上比纯参数更新（RL）最高提升3倍样本效率，减少70% KL散度，并缓解灾难性遗忘和塑性丧失问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统参数更新（如RL）会导致灾难性遗忘和塑性丧失，而纯上下文学习虽然灵活但性能不及参数更新。两种学习方式各有利弊，不应局限于单一模式。受人类System 1/2不同时间尺度学习的启发，作者希望融合两者优势。

Method: 提出Fast-Slow Training (FST)框架：慢权重——LLM模型参数，保持通用推理能力；快权重——优化后的上下文（prompt），通过文本反馈学习任务特定信息。训练时快权重快速吸收任务知识，慢权重保持稳定。

Result: 1) 样本效率最高提升3倍；2) 性能渐近线更高；3) KL散度降低70%，减轻灾难性遗忘；4) 保持塑性，后续任务适应更好；5) 在连续学习场景中持续习得新任务，而纯RL训练停滞。

Conclusion: FST有效融合了上下文学习（快）和参数更新（慢）的优势，为LLM提供了一种更高效、更鲁棒的学习范式，特别是在连续学习和防遗忘场景下具有显著优势。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are trained for downstream tasks by updating their parameters (e.g., via RL). However, updating parameters forces them to absorb task-specific information, which can result in catastrophic forgetting and loss of plasticity. In contrast, in-context learning with fixed LLM parameters can cheaply and rapidly adapt to task-specific requirements (e.g., prompt optimization), but cannot by itself typically match the performance gains available through updating LLM parameters. There is no good reason for restricting learning to being in-context or in-weights. Moreover, humans also likely learn at different time scales (e.g., System 1 vs 2). To this end, we introduce a fast-slow learning framework for LLMs, with model parameters as "slow" weights and optimized context as "fast" weights. These fast "weights" can learn from textual feedback to absorb the task-specific information, while allowing slow weights to stay closer to the base model and persist general reasoning behaviors. Fast-Slow Training (FST) is up to 3x more sample-efficient than only slow learning (RL) across reasoning tasks, while consistently reaching a higher performance asymptote. Moreover, FST-trained models remain closer to the base LLM (up to 70% less KL divergence), resulting in less catastrophic forgetting than RL-training. This reduced drift also preserves plasticity: after training on one task, FST trained models adapt more effectively to a subsequent task than parameter-only trained models. In continual learning scenarios, where task domains change on the fly, FST continues to acquire each new task while parameter-only RL stalls.

</details>


### [227] [Pion: A Spectrum-Preserving Optimizer via Orthogonal Equivalence Transformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12492)
*Kexuan Shi,Hanxuan Li,Zeju Qiu,Yandong Wen,Simon Buchholz,Weiyang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Pion是一种基于正交等价变换的保谱优化器，通过左右正交变换更新权重矩阵，在训练过程中保持奇异值不变，为LLM预训练和微调提供了稳定且有竞争力的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有优化器（如Adam、Muon）是加性优化器，可能改变权重矩阵的谱结构。作者希望设计一种能保持权重矩阵奇异值不变的优化方法，从而在调节权重矩阵几何结构的同时固定其谱范数。

Method: Pion通过左右正交变换更新每个权重矩阵，利用正交等价变换保持训练过程中奇异值不变，推导了更新规则并系统研究了设计选择和收敛性质。

Result: 实验结果表明，Pion在LLM预训练和微调中表现出稳定且有竞争力的性能，可作为标准优化器的替代方案。

Conclusion: Pion作为一种保谱优化器，通过正交变换实现了对权重矩阵几何结构的调控而保持谱范数固定，为LLM训练提供了新的优化范式。

Abstract: We introduce Pion, a spectrum-preserving optimizer for large language model (LLM) training based on orthogonal equivalence transformation. Unlike additive optimizers such as Adam and Muon, Pion updates each weight matrix through left and right orthogonal transformations, preserving its singular values throughout training. This yields an optimization mechanism that modulates the geometry of weight matrices while keeping their spectral norm fixed. We derive the Pion update rule, systematically examine its design choices, and analyze its convergence behavior along with several key properties. Empirical results show that Pion offers a stable and competitive alternative to standard optimizers for both LLM pretraining and finetuning.

</details>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [228] [ShardTensor: Domain Parallelism for Scientific Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11111)
*Corey Adams,Peter Harrington,Akshay Subramaniam,Mohammad Shoaib Abbas,Jaideep Pathak,Mike Pritchard,Sanjay Choudhry*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: ShardTensor是一种新的域并行化范式，通过将输入数据的空间维度与硬件约束解耦，实现了对任意规模输入数据的灵活扩展，在科学机器学习中支持高保真训练和推理，并展示了强扩展和弱扩展能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学机器学习在处理极端分辨率数据时面临扩展性挑战，现有方法要么无法扩展，要么会降低模型精度。虽然已有针对大规模空间数据的专用方法，但缺乏一个通用的、在设备批量大小为1的情况下对输入数据进行并行化的框架。

Method: 提出ShardTensor域并行范式，通过将输入数据的空间维度与硬件约束解耦，实现任意规模输入数据的灵活扩展，支持在训练和推理中进行强扩展和弱扩展。

Result: 在训练和推理中均展示了强扩展（降低延迟）和弱扩展（处理更大数据量）的能力，同时实现了多个维度的并行化，消除了极端规模输入下的SciML障碍。

Conclusion: ShardTensor为科学机器学习提供了一种通用的域并行化框架，能够突破硬件限制处理极端大规模空间数据，实现高保真训练和推理。

Abstract: Scientific Machine Learning (SciML) faces unique challenges for extreme-resolution data, with mitigations that often fail to scale or degrade the accuracy of trained models. While some specialized methods have achieved remarkable results in training models or performing inference on massive spatial datasets with bespoke techniques, there is no generalized framework for parallelization over input data below batch size one per device. In this work we introduce ShardTensor: a novel paradigm of domain parallelism that enables flexible scaling of input data to arbitrary sizes. By decoupling the spatial dimensionality of input data from hardware constraints, ShardTensor enables scientific machine learning workloads to reach new levels of high fidelity training and inference. We demonstrate both strong and weak scaling of workloads during training and inference, showing improved latency with strong scaling and demonstrating the capacity to process higher data sizes with weak scaling. Additionally, we demonstrate multiple dimensions of parallelization, removing barriers to SciML on extreme-scale inputs.

</details>


### [229] [ReCoVer: Resilient LLM Pre-Training System via Fault-Tolerant Collective and Versatile Workload](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11215)
*Ziyue Liu,Zhengyang Wang,Ruijie Zhang,Avinash Maurya,Hui Zhou,Paul Hovland,Sheng Di,Franck Cappello,Bogdan Nicolae,Zheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: ReCoVer是一个面向大语言模型预训练的弹性训练系统，通过保持每迭代微批次数量恒定这一核心不变性，确保梯度在随机意义上与无故障运行等价。系统采用三层解耦协议：容错集合通信、步内细粒度恢复和动态负载重分配，支持多种并行策略，在512 GPU上即使丢失256个GPU也能保持训练轨迹，相比检查点重启方案吞吐量提升2.23倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模GPU集群上预训练LLM时硬件故障已成常态，现有弹性训练框架要么只针对特定并行策略，要么会导致训练轨迹偏离无故障运行的结果，缺乏一种能保持训练轨迹一致性且并行策略无关的弹性训练系统。

Method: 提出三层解耦协议：(1)容错集合通信层，隔离故障跨副本传播；(2)步内细粒度恢复，保留迭代内进度并防止梯度损坏；(3)自适应负载策略，在幸存节点间动态重新分配微批次配额。设计上与并行策略无关，可直接集成到3D并行和HSDP中。

Result: 在512 GPU上，即使运行过程中丢失256个GPU，ReCoVer仍能保持与无故障参考一致的训练轨迹。相比检查点重启基线，有效吞吐量提升2.23倍，在234 GPU小时内多处理74.9%的token，且优势随时间扩大。

Conclusion: ReCoVer通过保持每迭代微批次数量不变的核心设计，实现了并行策略无关的弹性训练，在保证训练轨迹一致性的同时显著提升了故障恢复效率，为大模型大规模训练的可靠性提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Pre-training large language models on massive GPU clusters has made hardware faults routine rather than rare, driving the need for resilient training systems. Yet existing frameworks either focus on specific parallelism schemes or risk drifting away from a failure-free training trajectory. We propose ReCoVer, a resilient LLM pre-training system that upholds a single invariant: each iteration keeps the number of microbatches constant, ensuring per-iteration gradients remain stochastically equivalent to a failure-free run. The framework is organized as three decoupled protocol layers: (1) Fault-tolerant collectives that isolate faults from propagating across replicas; (2) in-step fine-grained recovery that preserves intra-iteration progress and prevents gradient corruption; (3) versatile-workload policy that dynamically redistributes microbatch quotas across the survivors. The design is parallelism-agnostic, integrating directly with both 3D parallelism and Hybrid Sharded Data Parallel (HSDP) as a drop-in substrate. We evaluate our implementation on end-to-end pre-training tasks for up to 512 GPUs, ReCoVer successfully preserves the training trajectory from a failure-free reference despite of 256 GPUs lost spread across the run. For comparison with checkpoint-and-restart baselines, ReCoVer demonstrates $2.23\times$ higher effective throughput after successive failures. This advantage results in ReCoVer processing 74.9% more tokens at 234 GPU-hours, with the gap widening as the training prolongs.

</details>


### [230] [Byzantine Consensus in Directed Graphs with Message Authentication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11309)
*Nitin H. Vaidya,Lewis Tseng*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文研究了有向通信网络中在消息认证机制下的共识问题，分别给出了同步系统中精确共识和异步系统中近似共识的充要条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有向通信网络中，节点之间的通信可能存在单向性，传统的共识条件（如完全连通或双向连通）不再适用。本文旨在在有消息认证（如数字签名）的环境下，找出有向图结构下实现共识的根本条件。

Method: 作者假设存在消息认证机制来验证消息完整性，在此基础上研究了同步系统（精确共识）和异步系统（近似共识）两种模型，通过理论分析推导出有向通信图上的必要条件和充分条件。

Result: 给出了同步精确共识和异步近似共识在有向通信图上的充要条件，明确了在有消息认证的场景下，什么样的图结构能够支撑共识达成。

Conclusion: 有消息认证机制时，有向网络中的共识问题可以在比传统假设更宽松的图结构下达成，研究结果为分布式系统中的容错共识设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We consider the problem of reaching consensus in communication networks that are modeled by directed graphs. We assume the existence of a message authentication mechanism (such as digital signatures) to verify the integrity of messages. We identify the necessary and sufficient conditions on the directed communication graph for the following problems to be solvable: (i) exact consensus in synchronous systems; and (ii) approximate consensus in asynchronous systems.

</details>


### [231] [MLCommons Chakra: Advancing Performance Benchmarking and Co-design using Standardized Execution Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11333)
*Srinivas Sridharan,Andy Balogh,Bradford M. Beckmann,Brian Coutinho,Louis Feng,Sheng Fu,Sanshan Gao,Mehryar Garakani,Taekyung Heo,David Kanter,Josh Ladd,Ziwei Li,Winston Liu,Changhai Man,Dan Mihailescu,Spandan More,Joongun Park,Ashwin Ramachandran,Vinay Ramakrishnaiah,Saeed Rashidi,Vijay Janapa Reddi,Puneet Sharma,Phio Tian,William Won,Hanjiang Wu,Huan Xu,Jinsun Yoo,Tushar Krishna*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Chakra 是一个开放的、可移植的分布式 AI/ML 工作负载性能基准测试与协同设计生态系统，核心是 Chakra 执行追踪（ET）图表示，并配套了收集、分析、生成和采用工具，已被 MLCommons 及多家行业巨头采用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI 创新的快速步伐需要一种敏捷方法来观察、复现和优化生产环境中分布式 ML 工作负载的行为，并支持高效的软硬件协同设计。

Method: 提出 Chakra 生态系统，核心是开放可互操作的图表示（Chakra ET），涵盖计算、内存、通信等关键操作及依赖、时序和资源约束；并配套工具链支持 ET 的收集、分析、生成和在不同模拟器/仿真器/回放工具中的采用。

Result: 在真实生产 AI 集群上收集了 Chakra ET 并进行了分析，通过实际案例验证了其价值。

Conclusion: Chakra 已被 MLCommons 采纳，并获得 NVIDIA、AMD、Meta 等多家行业领先企业的参与和贡献，表明其在产业界具有广泛影响力和实用性。

Abstract: The fast pace of artificial intelligence~(AI) innovation demands an agile methodology for observation, reproduction and optimization of distributed machine learning~(ML) workload behavior in production AI systems and enables efficient software-hardware~(SW-HW) co-design for future systems. We present Chakra, an open and portable ecosystem for performance benchmarking and co-design. The core component of Chakra is an open and interoperable graph-based representation of distributed AI/ML workloads, called Chakra execution trace~(ET). These ETs represent key operations, such as compute, memory, and communication, data and control dependencies, timing, and resource constraints. Additionally, Chakra includes a complementary set of tools and capabilities to enable the collection, analysis, generation, and adoption of Chakra ETs by a broad range of simulators, emulators, and replay tools. We present analysis of Chakra ETs collected on production AI clusters and demonstrate value via real-world case studies. Chakra has been adopted by MLCommons and has active contributions and engagement across the industry, including but not limited to NVIDIA, AMD, Meta, Keysight, HPE, and Scala, to name a few.

</details>


### [232] [The Illusion of Power Capping in LLM Decode: A Phase-Aware Energy Characterisation Across Attention Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11999)
*Bole Ma,Ayesha Afzal,Jan Eitzinger,Gerhard Wellein*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 论文揭示GPU功率封顶在LLM自回归解码阶段无效（实际功耗仅137-300W，远低于700W上限），并提出SM时钟锁定作为替代方案，可节约高达32%的解码能耗，同时识别了三种DVFS行为模式和新注意力机制的能量特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 证明当前GPU功率封顶在LLM生产服务中的自回归解码阶段是无效的，因为该阶段受内存带宽限制而非计算限制，功率封顶从未被触发，且固件时钟节流会干扰测量。

Method: 在NVIDIA H200 GPU上，对比四种注意力范式（GQA、MLA、Gated DeltaNet、Mamba2），测量自回归解码的实际功耗；提出SM时钟锁定替代功率封顶，并分析时钟锁定在不同架构下的能耗效果。

Result: 解码阶段实际功耗仅为137-300W（GPU标称700W），功率封顶从未触发；SM时钟锁定可恢复高达32%的解码能耗，且吞吐损失极小。此外，新注意力机制（如MLA、Mamba2）呈现“高预填充成本但高效解码”的能量模式，可在生产批次大小下将总请求能耗减半。

Conclusion: 功率封顶在LLM解码阶段是幻觉，SM时钟锁定是更优的能耗控制杠杆；未来GPU能耗优化应聚焦于内存带宽瓶颈和动态电压频率调整（DVFS）行为建模。

Abstract: Power capping is the standard GPU energy lever in LLM serving, and it appears to work: throughput drops, power readings fall, and energy budgets are met. We show the appearance is illusory for the phase that dominates production serving: autoregressive decode. Across four attention paradigms -- GQA, MLA, Gated DeltaNet, and Mamba2 -- on NVIDIA H200, decode draws only 137--300\,W on a 700\,W GPU; no cap ever triggers, because memory-bound decode saturates HBM bandwidth rather than compute and leaves power headroom untouched. Firmware-initiated clock throttling compounds the illusion: these deviations can corrupt any throughput measurement that attributes them to the cap. SM clock locking dissolves both confounds. By targeting the lever that is actually on the critical path, clock locking Pareto-dominates power capping universally, recovering up to 32\% of decode energy at minimal throughput loss. We identify three architecture-dependent DVFS behavioural classes and characterise a common energy pattern across novel attention replacements: a heavy prefill cost recouped by efficient decode, eventually halving total request energy relative to GQA at production batch sizes.

</details>


### [233] [ChunkFlow: Communication-Aware Chunked Prefetching for Layerwise Offloading in Distributed Diffusion Transformer Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11335)
*Han Meng,Danny Willow Liu,Dong Li*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出ChunkFlow，一种通信感知的块粒度卸载运行时，通过协同调度预取和集体通信，解决了扩散Transformer推理中层间卸载在PCIe节点上因通信争用导致的延迟暴露问题，在多种扩散Transformer上实现了最高1.28x的步时间加速，并提供了可调的内存-延迟权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层间卸载（layerwise offloading）能减少扩散Transformer推理的GPU内存占用，但其有效性依赖于预取延迟能被逐层计算隐藏。当每GPU计算量较小时，此假设不成立；此外在纯PCIe节点上，预取与跨GPU集体通信（如all-reduce、all-to-all）共享PCIe路径，产生争用，进一步暴露预取延迟。现有方案未解决此通信-预取冲突问题。

Method: 提出ChunkFlow：1）建立一阶分析模型，预测预取何时能被计算隐藏；2）设计通信感知的块粒度卸载运行时，自适应地让路给集体通信；3）平滑地在GPU内存与预取量之间进行权衡。

Result: 在三个代表性扩散Transformer上，使用两块H100 GPU通过PCIe连接，采用Ulysses序列并行：相比SGLang的层间卸载，步时间加速最高1.28x；相比无卸载基线，峰值GPU内存降低最高49%，且工作负载足够大时步时间几乎不变；在小工作负载场景下，可恢复接近零的步时间开销。

Conclusion: ChunkFlow通过通信感知的协同调度，有效解决了层间卸载在PCIe节点上面临的预取-通信争用问题，在减少GPU内存的同时保持了推理效率，并提供了灵活的内存-延迟权衡机制。

Abstract: Layerwise offloading reduces the GPU memory footprint of large diffusion transformer (DiT) inference by prefetching upcoming layers from host memory, but its effectiveness hinges on hiding prefetch latency behind per-layer computation. This assumption breaks down when the per-GPU compute workload is small. Moreover, on PCIe-only nodes, prefetch and inter-GPU collective communications such as all-reduce and all-to-all contend on the shared PCIe path, exposing prefetch latency even when compute would otherwise hide it. We revisit layerwise offloading as a co-scheduling problem between prefetch and communication, guided by a first-order analytical model that predicts when prefetch can be hidden by computation. Building on this model, we design ChunkFlow, a communication-aware, chunk-granular offloading runtime that adaptively yields to collective communication and smoothly trades GPU memory for prefetch volume. On three representative diffusion transformers running on two H100 GPUs over PCIe with Ulysses sequence parallelism, ChunkFlow delivers up to 1.28x step-time speedup over SGLang's existing layerwise offloading, reduces peak GPU memory by up to 49% over the no-offload baseline at near-identical step time once the workload is large enough, and exposes a tunable memory-latency tradeoff that recovers near-zero step-time overhead in the small-workload regime.

</details>


### [234] [GriNNder: Breaking the Memory Capacity Wall in Full-Graph GNN Training with Storage Offloading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11517)
*Jaeyong Song,Seongyeon Park,Hongsun Jang,Jaewon Jung,Hunseong Lim,Junguk Hong,Jinho Lee*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: GriNNder是首个利用存储设备（NVMe SSD）在单GPU上实现大规模全图GNN训练的系统，通过结构化存储卸载框架（SSO）管理GPU-主机-存储层次，相比现有方法最高加速9.78倍，性能可比肩分布式系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全图GNN训练通常需要多GPU/服务器，硬件和通信成本高昂；现有单服务器方法受限于GPU和主机内存容量，无法处理大规模图数据。

Method: 提出结构化存储卸载（SSO）框架，包含三个核心组件：(1) 基于跨分区依赖观察的逐分区缓存策略；(2) 消除冗余存储操作的梯度重聚策略；(3) 降低现有图划分器内存需求的轻量级划分方案。

Result: 在多种模型和数据集上，相比最先进基线最高加速9.78倍，吞吐量可与分布式系统相当，实现了单GPU上先前不可行的大规模全图训练。

Conclusion: 通过利用NVMe SSD的高带宽和大容量特性，结合针对GNN访问模式设计的存储层级管理机制，GriNNder有效解决了内存受限下的全图训练瓶颈。

Abstract: Full-graph training of graph neural networks (GNNs) is widely used as it enables direct validation of algorithmic improvements by preserving complete neighborhood information. However, it typically requires multiple GPUs or servers, incurring substantial hardware and inter-device communication costs. While existing single-server methods reduce infrastructure requirements, they remain constrained by GPU and host memory capacity as graph sizes increase. To address this limitation, we introduce GriNNder, which is the first work to leverage storage devices to enable full-graph training even with limited memory. Because modern NVMe SSDs offer multi-terabyte capacities and bandwidths exceeding 10 GB/s, they provide an appealing option when memory resources are scarce. Yet, directly applying storage-based methods from other domains fails to address the unique access patterns and data dependencies in full-graph GNN training. GriNNder tackles these challenges by structured storage offloading (SSO), a framework that manages the GPU-host-storage hierarchy through coordinated cache, (re)gather, and bypass mechanisms. To realize the framework, we devise (i) a partition-wise caching strategy for host memory that exploits the observation on cross-partition dependencies, (ii) a regathering strategy for gradient computation that eliminates redundant storage operations, and (iii) a lightweight partitioning scheme that mitigates the memory requirements of existing graph partitioners. In experiments performed over various models and datasets, GriNNder achieves up to 9.78x speedup over state-of-the-art baselines and throughput comparable to distributed systems, enabling previously infeasible large-scale full-graph training even on a single GPU.

</details>


### [235] [State Twins: An Off-Chain Substrate for Agentic Reasoning over Decentralized Finance Protocols](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11522)
*Ian C. Moore*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出State Twin——一种类型化、内存级、可重放的链上AMM池副本，作为DeFi协议上智能体推理的底层基础设施。它解耦了链上时间与推理过程，支持分叉、回放、分支和反事实推演，并在DeFiPy v2中以开源形式实现，同时作为LLM工具暴露类型化分析原语。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体DeFi架构将推理与链上时间紧密耦合，每次"what-if"查询都会产生新的RPC读取或真实交易，使得智能体的有效动作空间受限于区块确认延迟和Gas费用。作者认为这是结构性而非性能问题，缺失的是离线推理底层设施。

Method: 将每个AMM家族（Uniswap V2/V3、Balancer、Stableswap）形式化为离散时间受控动力系统；证明双生子与链上状态之间偏差的定量保真度上界；在DeFiPy v2中实现开放架构，并提供Model Context Protocol服务器，将类型化分析原语暴露为LLM工具。

Result: 同一原语（一个Python类、一种调用模式）无需修改即可服务于notebook量化分析、回测和LLM智能体三种场景。示例中，一次链上RPC读取即可在亚秒级墙钟时间内，在N个独立内存双生子下模拟不同的价格冲击场景。

Conclusion: 贡献在于底层基础设施本身，而非特定智能体。这项工作明确了智能体化DeFi底层设施应有的规范形态。

Abstract: We introduce the State Twin: a typed, in-memory, replayable replica of an on-chain automated market maker (AMM) pool that serves as a substrate for agentic reasoning over decentralized finance (DeFi) protocols. Agentic DeFi stacks today couple reasoning to chain time, since every "what if?" query incurs a new RPC read or a real transaction, so the agent's effective action space is bounded by block confirmation latency and gas. We argue this coupling is a structural problem rather than a performance one, and that the missing layer is an off-chain substrate that preserves the protocol's exact mathematics while admitting the operations on-chain state cannot: forking, replay, branching, counterfactual rollout. We formalize each AMM family (Uniswap V2, V3, Balancer, Stableswap) as a discrete-time controlled dynamical system, prove a quantitative fidelity bound on the divergence between twin and chain, and give the open architecture used in DeFiPy v2, an open-source Python toolkit that ships the State Twin substrate and a reference Model Context Protocol server exposing typed analytical primitives as LLM tools. The same primitive (i.e., one Python class, one calling pattern) serves a notebook quant, a backtest, and an LLM agent without modification. We close with a fork-and-evaluate worked example: a single live RPC read seeds N independent in-memory twins under distinct price-shock scenarios, in sub-second wall-clock time. The contribution is the substrate, not a particular agent, which is what the specification of what an agentic DeFi substrate must look like

</details>


### [236] [NAVIS: Concurrent Search and Update with Low Position-Seeking Overhead in On-SSD Graph-Based Vector Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11523)
*Jaeyong Song,Hongsun Jang,Changmin Shin,Seongyeon Park,Yong Jae Ryoo,Seo Jin Park,Jinho Lee*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: NAVIS通过选择性向量读取、动态入口图更新和入口图感知边列表缓存三种技术，显著降低了基于SSD的图向量搜索系统中的位置寻找开销，在保持高召回率的同时提升了插入和并发搜索吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于磁盘的图向量搜索系统在高维工作负载下难以维持并发搜索和更新的高吞吐量，根本原因是每次更新都需要执行位置寻找（position seeking）这一全图遍历操作，其成本远高于搜索查询，且被打包布局和静态入口图两大系统性问题进一步放大。

Method: 提出了三种关键技术：(1) 布局支持的向量选择性读取，打破打包页面的耦合但不损失局部性；(2) 动态轻量级入口图更新机制，重用并发更新产生的遍历信息；(3) 入口图感知的边列表缓存，将容量集中在靠近刷新入口点的高重用路径上。

Result: 在多个大规模高维基准测试中，NAVIS将平均插入吞吐量提升高达2.74倍，平均并发搜索吞吐量提升高达1.37倍，平均搜索延迟降低高达25.26%。

Conclusion: NAVIS通过针对性解决位置寻找开销问题，有效提升了基于SSD的图向量搜索系统在并发更新和搜索场景下的性能表现。

Abstract: On-disk graph-based vector search (GVS) has become the dominant approach for serving large-scale vector databases at high recall, but prior systems struggle to sustain concurrent search and update throughput on high-dimensional workloads. We find the main cause of this in position seeking, a full graph traversal that every update performs to locate neighbors before linking the new vector into the graph. Position seeking is fundamentally heavier than a search query, and its cost is further amplified by two systemic limitations of current GVS systems, packed layouts that couple every edge fetch to a full vector load, and a static entrance graph whose entry points drift away from newly inserted regions as updates accumulate.
  We present NAVIS, an on-SSD GVS system that drives down position-seeking overhead through (i) a layout-supported selective vector read that breaks the packed-page coupling without losing its locality benefits, (ii) a dynamic lightweight entrance graph update mechanism that reuses traversal information already produced by concurrent updates, and (iii) an entrance graph-aware edgelist cache that concentrates capacity on high-reuse paths near refreshed entry points. Across multiple large-scale high-dimensional benchmarks, NAVIS enhances average insertion throughput by up to 2.74x and average concurrent search throughput by up to 1.37x while reducing average search latency by up to 25.26%.

</details>


### [237] [GraphFlash: Enabling Fast and Elastic Graph Processing on Serverless Infrastructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11631)
*Chen Zhao,Parsa Poorsistani,Mohammad Goudarzi,Tawfiq Islam,Adel N. Toosi*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: GraphFlash是一个基于Serverless架构的快速弹性图处理框架，通过子图中心编程模型、共享外部存储、分区感知键聚合等优化，在多种图算法和数据集上比现有Serverless系统快127倍、资源消耗降低98%，同时匹配传统分布式框架的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图处理系统依赖静态集群，弹性差、资源利用率低；而Serverless图系统的状态管理低效且通过外部存储通信开销大，亟需一种兼具弹性与高性能的图处理方案。

Method: GraphFlash采用子图中心编程模型，利用共享外部存储实现无状态细粒度函数执行；支持旋转模式（资源受限）和固定模式（资源充足）；引入分区感知键聚合、函数内分区共置、超步感知激活等系统级优化。

Result: 在多种图算法和数据集上，GraphFlash比现有Serverless系统快127倍，资源消耗降低98%；在资源受限时仍实现48倍加速和99.97%成本降低；性能可匹配传统分布式框架。

Conclusion: GraphFlash通过精心设计的系统优化，使Serverless图处理变得实用且高效，兼顾弹性伸缩与高性能。

Abstract: Graph processing systems are essential for analyzing large-scale data with complex relationships, yet most existing frameworks rely on statically provisioned clusters, resulting in poor elasticity and inefficient resource utilization under dynamic workloads. Serverless computing offers automatic scaling and fine-grained billing, but existing serverless graph systems suffer from performance limitations due to inefficient state management and high communication overhead through external storage. We present GraphFlash, a fast and elastic graph processing framework built on serverless infrastructure. GraphFlash adopts a subgraph-centric programming model and leverages shared external storage for coordination and communication, enabling stateless, fine-grained function execution. It supports two execution modes: rotating mode for resource-constrained environments and pinned mode for higher performance when resources are sufficient. To address serverless limitations, GraphFlash introduces system-level optimizations, including partition-aware key aggregation, intra-function partition co-location, and superstep-aware activation. Across multiple graph algorithms and datasets, GraphFlash outperforms existing serverless-compatible systems by up to 127x in execution time and reduces resource consumption by up to 98% under higher-resource configurations, while matching the performance of traditional distributed frameworks on large workloads. Even with limited resources, it achieves up to 48x speedup and 99.97% cost reduction over prior serverless solutions, demonstrating that GraphFlash makes serverless graph processing practical and performant.

</details>


### [238] [Trade-offs in Decentralized Agentic AI Discovery Across the Compute Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11839)
*Patrizio Dazzi,Emanuele Carlini,Matteo Mordacchini,Saul Urso*

Main category: cs.DC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨云、边缘和间歇性连接域部署的智能体系统需要有效的发现机制，而基于DHT的结构化覆盖网络正成为去中心化智能体发现的设计方向，因此需要研究不同覆盖网络的适用性。

Method: 在共享控制平面框架内，选取4096节点的静态场景和含节点加入离开（churn）的动态场景作为基准测试，对比Chord、Pastry和Kademlia三种结构化覆盖网络在智能体发现任务上的性能。

Result: 三种覆盖网络在发现可靠性、启动行为和控制平面开销上表现出不同的权衡特性，适用于边缘到云端的不同部署环境。

Conclusion: 研究为在边缘到云环境下选择结构化覆盖网络进行智能体发现提供了清晰的优化操作点参考。

Abstract: Agentic systems deployed across the compute continuum need discovery mechanisms that remain effective across cloud, edge, and intermittently connected domains. In some emerging agentic architectures, decentralized discovery is already an active design direction, placing DHT-based lookup on the path toward agent directories. This paper studies the trade-offs among major structured-overlay families for agent discovery, comparing Chord, Pastry, and Kademlia as candidate indexing substrates within a shared control-plane framework. Using a benchmark subset centered on a 4096-node stationary comparison and a representative 4096-node churn benchmark, the paper characterizes how discovery reliability, startup behavior, and control-plane overhead vary across these overlays. The goal is to clarify the operating points they expose for agent discovery across edge-to-cloud environments.

### [239] [AB-Sparse: Sparse Attention with Adaptive Block Size for Accurate and Efficient Long-Context Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12110)
*Di Liu,Ruitian Wang,Chen Chen,Mingliang Gong,Yongjie Yuan,Han Zhao,Yu Feng,Quan Chen,Minyi Guo*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出AB-Sparse，一种无需训练的自适应块稀疏注意力框架，通过为不同注意力头分配不同块大小来提升精度，并利用块质心量化减少内存开销，配合自定义GPU内核实现高效执行，在保持吞吐量的前提下将精度提升高达5.43%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有块稀疏注意力方法为所有注意力头分配统一块大小，忽略了不同注意力头对块粒度的敏感度差异，导致精度次优。

Method: 提出AB-Sparse框架：(1)轻量级自适应块大小分配，为不同注意力头分配不同块大小；(2)无损块质心量化以补偿额外内存开销；(3)支持可变块大小的自定义GPU内核加速。

Result: 相比现有块稀疏注意力基线，精度提升最高达5.43%，且无吞吐量损失。

Conclusion: 注意力头对块粒度的敏感性存在显著差异，自适应分配块大小可以在不牺牲效率的前提下有效提升稀疏注意力精度。

Abstract: As large language models scale to longer contexts, loading the growing KV cache during attention computation becomes a critical bottleneck. Previous work has shown that attention computation is dominated by a small subset of tokens. This motivates block sparse attention methods that partition the KV cache into fixed-size blocks and selectively compute attention over those blocks exhibiting high importance. However, these methods assign a uniform block size across all attention heads, implicitly assuming homogeneous behavior throughout the model. Our analysis reveals that this assumption is flawed: attention heads exhibit widely varying sensitivity to block granularity, and uniformity leads to suboptimal accuracy. We present AB-Sparse, a training-free algorithm-system co-designed framework that improves accuracy while preserving throughput. AB-Sparse introduces lightweight adaptive block size allocation across attention heads to improve accuracy. To compensate for the additional memory overhead, it further employs lossless block centroid quantization. In addition, custom GPU kernels are developed to support efficient execution with variable block sizes. Evaluation results demonstrate that AB-Sparse achieves an accuracy improvement of up to 5.43% over existing block sparse attention baselines without throughput overhead.

</details>


### [240] [NCCLZ: Compression-Enabled GPU Collectives with Decoupled Quantization and Entropy Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12396)
*Jiamin Wang,Zhijing Ye,Xiaodong Yu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: NCCLZ提出一种解耦量化与熵编码的GPU集合通信压缩框架，将量化放在接口层、熵编码嵌入NCCL原语，通过轻量级选择器自适应编码策略并实现压缩与通信重叠，相比NCCL最高加速9.65倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有集合通信库（如NCCL）在大消息传输时性能受限，而基于压缩的改进方案存在依赖MPI栈无法充分利用NCCL、缺乏熵编码、或压缩器与通信原语耦合过紧等问题，导致压缩率、灵活性和计算通信重叠能力不足。

Method: 将量化（quantization）与熵编码（entropy coding）解耦，量化置于接口层，熵编码嵌入NCCL原语内部；设计轻量级设备端选择器自适应选择编码策略；实现压缩过程与通信过程的重叠以降低暴露开销。

Result: 在科学数据集、训练梯度和合成工作负载上，相比NCCL最高获得9.65倍加速，相比已有压缩辅助集合库最高提升3.34倍。

Conclusion: 解耦量化与熵编码的分层集成策略能有效提升GPU集合通信的压缩效率与灵活性，同时通过计算通信重叠显著降低开销。

Abstract: Collective communication is a major bottleneck for multi-node GPU workloads in scientific computing and distributed deep learning, especially when inter-node bandwidth is limited. Although NCCL provides optimized GPU-centric collectives, large messages can still dominate end-to-end performance. Existing compression-enabled collective libraries either rely on MPI-based stacks that cannot fully exploit NCCL, omit entropy coding, or tightly couple full compressors with communication primitives, limiting compression ratio, flexibility, and communication-computation overlap. This paper presents NCCLZ, a compression-enabled GPU collectives that decouples quantization and entropy coding and integrates them at different layers of the stack. NCCLZ places quantization at the interface, embeds entropy coding into NCCL primitives, uses a lightweight device-side selector to choose coding strategies, and overlaps compression with communication to reduce exposed overhead. Experiments on scientific datasets, training gradients, and synthetic workloads show up to 9.65x speedup over NCCL and up to 3.34x improvement over prior compression-assisted collective libraries.

</details>

### [241] [A Fast and Energy-Efficient Latch-Based Memristive Analog Content-Addressable Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11847)
*Paul-Philipp Manea,Aishwarya Natarajan,Jim Ignowski,John Paul Strachan,Luca Buonanno*

Main category: cs.ET

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于强臂锁存忆阻器(SALM)的模拟内容可寻址存储器(aCAM)单元，通过动态电流竞争比较器替代传统静态分压，实现了高再生增益、内建锁存和近零静态搜索功耗，相比传统6T2M架构在保持精度的同时显著降低了能耗并提升了可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统6T2M aCAM架构存在静态搜索功耗大、电压增益有限以及匹配线串扰严重等问题，制约了模拟精度和阵列可扩展性，亟需一种新型电路设计来突破这些瓶颈。

Method: 提出SALM aCAM单元，用动态电流竞争比较器替代静态电压分压；支持可扩展的顺序/并行锁存共享；开发基于22nm FD-SOI SPICE查表的行为模型；设计数据集感知优化框架，暴露能量-延迟权衡。

Result: 相比6T2M，SALM在相同延迟下读能量降低33%，消除了增益和串扰限制；在代表性负载上可实现3倍延迟下50%的能量降低；在高维数据集上保持接近软件的精度，而基线设计因增益不足和累积串扰而性能下降。

Conclusion: SALM架构有效解决了传统aCAM的可扩展性和能效瓶颈，为大规模边缘AI和嵌入式智能应用中的关联计算提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Analog content-addressable memories (aCAMs) based on memristors provide a promising pathway toward energy-efficient large-scale associative computing for Edge AI and embedded intelligence applications. They have been successfully applied to decision-tree inference and extend the capabilities of compute-in-memory (CIM) architectures beyond conventional vector-matrix multiplication. However, conventional designs such as the 6T2M architecture suffer from static search power, limited voltage gain, and pronounced match-line crosstalk, constraining analog precision and scalability. We introduce a strong-arm latched memristor (SALM) aCAM cell that replaces static voltage division with a dynamic current-race comparator, enabling high regenerative gain, intrinsic result latching, and near-zero static search power. Compared to 6T2M, SALM reduces read energy by 33% at identical latency while eliminating the gain and crosstalk limitations that prevent 6T2M from scaling to large arrays. SALM further enables scalable sequential and parallel latch sharing, and a dataset-aware optimization framework exposes an explicit energy-latency tradeoff, achieving up to 50% energy reduction at 3x latency across representative workloads. To enable architectural exploration, we develop a circuit-accurate behavioral model derived from SPICE lookup tables in 22 nm FD-SOI technology, capturing match-line dynamics and crosstalk. Integrated into the X-TIME decision-tree compiler, this framework demonstrates that SALM maintains near-software accuracy for high-dimensional datasets, whereas baseline designs degrade due to limited gain and cumulative crosstalk.

</details>
